inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> partially</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> offset by</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">inflation across several food costs, primarily dairy,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">tortillas,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">salsa, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">beans</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> and</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> rice</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">a mix shift towards Garlic Guajillo Steak, a limited time menu item</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Restaurant level operating margin was 2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">5.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">compared to</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">20.7</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">first</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter of 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. The </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">improvement</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> was</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> primarily </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">due to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">the benefit of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">sales leverage</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> and, to a lesser extent, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">lower avocado prices and lower delivery expense due to lower delivery volumes</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> These decreases were partially offset by higher </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">inflation across several food costs </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">and to a lesser extent, wage inflation.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

		</p>

		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Digital sales</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> represent food and beverage revenue generated through the Chipotle website, Chipotle app or third-party delivery aggregators. Digital sales </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">include revenue deferrals associated with Chipotle Rewards. </font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">In-restaurant sales </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">represent food and beverage revenue generated on-premise. In-restaurant sales includes revenue deferrals associated with Chipotle Rewards. </font></p></td></tr></table></div></div><div style="margin-left:36pt;margin-right:36pt;">

		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 10pt"><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Conference Call Details</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Chipotle</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">will</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> host a conference call on </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">Tuesday</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">, &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">April</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> &nbsp;2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">5</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">, 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> at 4:30 PM Eastern time</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">discuss </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">first</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> quarter 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> financial results as well as provide a business update for the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">second</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">The</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">conference</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> call can be accessed live over the phone by dialing 1-888-317-6003</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> or for international callers by dialing 1-412-317-6061</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> and use code: </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">3598907</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">. The call will be webcast live from the company's website on the investor relations page at ir.chipotle.com/events. An archived webcast will be available approximately one hour after the end of the call.</font>

		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">About Chipotle</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">Chipotle Mexican Grill, Inc. (NYSE: CMG) is cultivating a better world by serving responsibly sourced, classically-cooked, real food with wholesome ingredients without artificial colors, flavors or preservatives. Chipotle had </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">over</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">3,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">00</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> restaurants as of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">March</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> &nbsp;3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">, 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">, in the United States, Canada, the United Kingdom, France and Germany and is the only restaurant company of its size that owns and operates all its restaurants. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">Chipotle is ranked on the Fortune 500 and is recognized on the 2022 list for Fortune&#x2019;s Most Admired Companies. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">With </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">over</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">100</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">,000 em</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">ployees passionate about providing a great guest experience, Chipotle is a longtime leader and innovator in the fo</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">od industry. Chipotle is committed to making its food more accessible to everyone while continuing to be a brand with a demonstrated purpose as it leads the way in digital, technology and sustainable business practices. For more information or to place an order online, visit </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#C08C19;background-color: #FFFFFF;">WWW.CHIPOTLE.COM</font><font style="display: inline;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Forward-Looking Statements</font>

These statements are subject to risks and uncertainties that could cause actual results to differ materially from those described in the statements, including but not limited to: uncertainty regarding the resurgence of COVID-19 infections</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">and its ultimate impact on our business; the impact of competition, including from sources outside the restaurant industry; the financial impact of increasing our average hourly wages; the impact of federal, state or local government regulations relating to our employees, employment practices, restaurant design and construction, and the sale of food or alcoholic beverages; our ability to achieve our planned growth, such as the availability of suitable new restaurant sites and the availability of construction materials and contractors; increases in ingredient and other operating costs due </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">to inflation, global conflicts, climate change, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">our Food </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">w</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">ith Integrity philosophy, tariffs or trade restrictions and supply shortages; the uncertainty of our ability to achieve expected levels of comparable restaurant sales due to factors such as changes in consumers' perceptions of our brand, including as a result of actual or rumored food safety concerns or other negative publicity, decreased consumer spending (including as a result of higher inflation, mass layoffs, fear of possible recession and higher energy prices), or the inability to increase menu prices or realize the benefits of menu price increases; risks associated with our digital business, including risks arising from our reliance on third party delivery services; risks relating to litigation, including possible governmental actions </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">and potentially class action litigation </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">related to food safety incidents</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">, cybersecurity incidents,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> employment</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> or privacy</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> laws, advertising claims or other matters; 		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;;font-size: 8pt"><font style="display: inline;font-size:8pt;"></font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 3pt;text-align:center;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">CHIPOTLE MEXICAN GRILL, INC.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 3pt;text-align:center;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">RECONCILIATION OF NON-GAAP FINANCIAL MEASURES</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:13pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<a name="_Hlk22568764"></a><font style="display: inline;">The following tables provide a reconciliation of non-GAAP financial measures presented in the text above to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">Adjusted net income is net income excluding expenses related to </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">restaurant asset impairment, corporate restructuring, </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">certain </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">legal proceedings, stock-</font><font style="display: inline;">based compensation modification expense, unrealized gains on equity investments, </font><font style="display: inline;">separation costs, </font><font style="display: inline;">and certain other costs. Adjusted general and administrative expense is general and administrative expense excluding transformation expenses, </font><font style="display: inline;">certain </font><font style="display: inline;">legal proceedings, stock-based compensation modification expense, </font><font style="display: inline;">separation costs, </font><font style="display: inline;">and certain other costs. The adjusted effective income tax rate is the effective income tax rate adjusted to reflect the after tax impact of non-GAAP adjustments. Restaurant Level Operating Margin, a non-GAAP financial measure, is equal to the revenues generated by our restaurants less their direct operating costs which consist of food, beverage and packaging, labor, occupancy and other operating costs. This performance measure primarily includes the costs that restaurant level managers can directly control and excludes other costs that are essential to conduct our business. Management uses restaurant level operating margin as a measure of restaurant performance. Management believes restaurant level operating margin is useful to investors in that it highlights trends in our core business that may not otherwise be apparent to investors when relying solely on GAAP financial measures. We present these non-GAAP measures in order to facilitate meaningful evaluation of our operating performance across periods. These adjustments are intended to provide greater transparency of underlying performance and to allow investors to evaluate our business on the same basis as our management, which uses these non-GAAP measures in evaluating the company&#x2019;s performance. Our adjusted net income, adjusted diluted earnings per share, adjusted general and administrative expenses, adjusted effective income tax rate and restaurant level operating margin measures may not be comparable to other companies&#x2019; adjusted measures. These adjustments are not necessarily indicative of what our actual financial performance would have been during the periods presented and should be viewed in addition to, and not as an alternative to, our results prepared in accordance with GAAP. Further details regarding these adjustments are included in the tables below.</font>
		</p>
